7	ed/716310	2144624	txt_reader	-	txt_reader (4)	COMPLETED	0	-	-	2	-	-	2 GB	1	2026-01-28 15:20:30.309	2026-01-28 15:20:30.450	2026-01-28 15:20:32.389	2.1s	1.2s	-	21.2%	0.0%	3.6 MB	7.2 MB	3.6 MB	7.2 MB	6.8 MB	19.2 KB	897	34	8 KB	24 KB	16	0	-	/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/work/ed/716310780a2c0448bab3b121c2405e	
    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_003.txt'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/readers/txt_reader.py" 'EV_003.txt' 'utf-16' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] txt_reader exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/readers/txt_reader.py" 'EV_003.txt' 'utf-16'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_txt_tree.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/quest_analyzer.py" 'EV_007_txt_tree.parquet' '['\''POS*'\'', '\''NEG*'\'', '\''NEU*'\'', {'\''x-labels'\'': ('\''samList'\'', ['\''Valence'\'', '\''Arousal'\'']), '\''y-max'\'': 9, '\''data'\'': '\''SAM.Choice1.Value'\''}]' 'sam' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"

        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/quest_analyzer.py" 'EV_008_txt_tree.parquet' '[{'\''x-labels'\'': ('\''bisBasList'\'', ['\''Familie'\'', '\''Nervosität'\'', '\''Anstrengung'\'', '\''Ausdauer'\'', '\''Neugier'\'', '\''Kleidung'\'', '\''Energie'\'', '\''Kritikempf.'\'', '\''Zielstrebig'\'', '\''Spaßsuche'\'', '\''Zeitmanagem.'\'', '\''Chancen'\'', '\''Sorge'\'', '\''Spannung'\'', '\''Impulsiv'\'', '\''Unruhe'\'', '\''Verhalten'\'', '\''Berührbar'\'', '\''Fehlersorge'\'', '\''Abwechslung'\'', '\''Hartnäckig'\'', '\''Angstfrei'\'', '\''Wettbewerb'\'', '\''Fehlerangst'\'']), '\''y-labels'\'': ['\''gar nicht'\'', '\''eher nicht'\'', '\''eher'\'', '\''genau'\''], '\''data'\'': '\''bisBas.Choice1.Value'\''}]' 'bisbas' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"

            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_txt_tree_sam.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)

        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"

        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log

        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_003_txt_tree_ea11.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_003_txt_tree_ea11.parquet' '*ea113.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_002_txt_tree_sam.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging

        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"

        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_002_txt_tree_sam.parquet' '*sam3.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_002_txt_tree_ea11.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_002_txt_tree_ea11.parquet' '*ea111.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_002_txt_tree_ea11.parquet' '*ea111.parquet'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_sam_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_007_sam_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_007' 'EV_007_sam' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] plotter exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_007_sam_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_007' 'EV_007_sam'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_sam_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_004_sam_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_004' 'EV_004_sam' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] plotter exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_xdf.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_004_xdf.parquet' 'type:NIRS.fif' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_004_xdf.parquet' 'type:NIRS.fif'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_003_xdf5_extr.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_003_xdf5_extr.parquet' '*extr2.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_003_xdf5_extr.parquet' '*extr2.parquet'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_xdf4_extr.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_007_xdf4_extr.parquet' '*extr4.fif' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_008_xdf3_log_tddr_lin_filt_epochs.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/group_analyzer.py" 'EV_008_xdf3_log_tddr_lin_filt_epochs.parquet' '{"Left PFC": ["re:^[12]-"], "Right PFC": ["re:^[34]-"]}' '0.5' 'ROI' ''\''HbO2 Change (μM)'\''' 'hbc' '5.0' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] group_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/group_analyzer.py" 'EV_008_xdf3_log_tddr_lin_filt_epochs.parquet' '{"Left PFC": ["re:^[12]-"], "Right PFC": ["re:^[34]-"]}' '0.5' 'ROI' ''\''HbO2 Change (μM)'\''' 'hbc' '5.0'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda1.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda2.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda3.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda1.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda2.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda3.parquet' 'eda_concat' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] concatenating_processor exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda1.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda2.parquet' 'EV_007_xdf4_extr1_filt_epochs_eda3.parquet' 'eda_concat'
    fi
    	-

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv.parquet' '*hrv3.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)

    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)

        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}

        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"

            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_eda_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_007_eda_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_007' 'EV_007_eda' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] plotter exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_007_eda_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_007' 'EV_007_eda'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_hrv_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_007_hrv_concat.parquet' 'NEU' '0.6' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv1.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv2.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv3.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv1.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv2.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv3.parquet' 'hrv_concat' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] concatenating_processor exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv1.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv2.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr2_filt_peaks_epochs_hrv3.parquet' 'hrv_concat'
    fi

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)

        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)

        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] concatenating_processor exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_hbc_fai_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_007_hbc_fai_concat.parquet' 'NEU' '0.3' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_002_hbc_fai_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_002_hbc_fai_concat.parquet' 'NEU' '0.3' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_hbc_fai_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/plotter.py" 'EV_004_hbc_fai_concat.parquet' '/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/EV_004' 'EV_004_hbc_fai' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] plotter exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_002_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_002_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica.parquet' '*ica_cleaned.fif' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else

    fi

        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}

        while IFS= read -r line; do

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_003_fai.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_003_fai.parquet' 'NEU' '0.5' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_007_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/asymmetry_analyzer.py" 'EV_007_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3.parquet' '[('\''F3'\'', '\''F4'\'')]' 'log' 'alpha' '0.4' 'None' 'psd_fai' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] asymmetry_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/asymmetry_analyzer.py" 'EV_007_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3.parquet' '[('\''F3'\'', '\''F4'\'')]' 'log' 'alpha' '0.4' 'None' 'psd_fai'

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/utils/file_finder.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd.parquet' '*psd3.parquet' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] file_finder exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd1_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd2_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3_psd_fai.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd1_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd2_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3_psd_fai.parquet' 'psd_fai_concat' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] concatenating_processor exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/processors/concatenating_processor.py" 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd1_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd2_psd_fai.parquet' 'EV_004_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3_psd_fai.parquet' 'psd_fai_concat'
    fi

    #!/bin/bash
    
    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_psd_concat.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)
    
    # Run processing with logging
    if [ -n "$PARTICIPANT_ID" ]; then
        LOG_FILE="/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../EV_results/${PARTICIPANT_ID}/${PARTICIPANT_ID}_pipeline.log"
        TEMP_OUT=$(mktemp)
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_004_psd_concat.parquet' 'NEU' '10.0' 2>&1 | tee "$TEMP_OUT"
        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') $line" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi
        exit $EXIT_CODE
    else
        /home/gutt/EV_venv/bin/python3 -u "/mnt/emotiview/repoShaggy/EmotiViewPrivate/EV_analysis/../../AnalysisToolbox/Python/analyzers/relative_analyzer.py" 'EV_004_psd_concat.parquet' 'NEU' '10.0'
    fi

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_004_fai.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
    PARTICIPANT_ID=$(echo "$INPUT_FILE" | grep -oE '^[A-Za-z]+_[0-9]+' | head -1)

        EXIT_CODE=${PIPESTATUS[0]}
        
        # Add timestamp to each line before appending to log
        while IFS= read -r line; do

        done < "$TEMP_OUT"
        rm -f "$TEMP_OUT"
        
        if [ $EXIT_CODE -ne 0 ]; then
            echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
            echo "$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S') [ERROR] relative_analyzer exit code $EXIT_CODE" >> "$LOG_FILE"
        fi

    # Extract participant ID from input filename (pattern like EV_002_*)
    INPUT_FILE=$(basename "'EV_008_xdf4_extr4_reref_filt_ica_cleaned_epochs_psd3.parquet'" | sed "s/'//g")
